To use it, start from the rightmost digit, double every second digit, and if the result is greater than 9, subtract 9. Sum all the digits (both doubled and undoubled) and check if the total sum is divisible by 10. If it is, the number is valid. ↵ ID X and Y ‎<This message was edited>
